F04:0053                                                   ; 2nd Nybble + 2 Bytes = 999999 Gold
F04:0054           endif
F04:0055           ;

F04:0059           endif
F04:0060           ;

               S13:0000E0A4:  4E 71
F04:0064           nop 
               S13:0000E0A6:  4E 71
F04:0065           endif

F04:0071           ;nop                                     ; with nops
F04:0072           ;endr
F04:0073                                                   ; (i) $70F0.w: Skip SubRoutine to Load Plane A Map to C000-CFFF
F04:0074                                                   ; (i) $70FE.w: Skip SubRoutine to Load Plane B Map to E000-EFFF

               S50:000A4C98:  B2 BC 00 0A 0E 00

               S50:000A4C9E:  67 22

               S50:000A4CA0:  B2 BC 00 0A 18 E7

               S50:000A4CB8:  B2 BC 00 0A 18 B8

F10:0005       cc_close            equ $00     ; Closes the textbox

F10:0007                                       ; format: 01.b 0RGB.w
F10:0008       cc_textOrange       equ $01A0
F10:0009       cc_textWhite        equ $0180
F10:0010       cc_fast             equ $02     ; Changes the write speed to 'fast'
F10:0011       cc_speed            equ $03     ; Changes the write speed to given value,
F10:0012                                       ; format 03 value.b: 00=fastest, 09=slowest
F10:0013       
F10:0014       cc_margin           equ $04     ; sets textbox margin
F10:0015                                       ; format 04 value.b, where value equals value*tilewidth=8 pixels
F10:0016       
F10:0017       cc_wait             equ $05     ; Displays arrow and waits for user input
F10:0018       cc_jump             equ $06     ; Jumps to a text location
F10:0019                                       ; format: 06.b pointer.w
F10:0020       cc_lock             equ $07     ; disables fast forward of text
F10:0021       cc_newline          equ $09     ; Starts a new line in the textbox

F13:0006       textData_Dialogues:
F13:0007       
F13:0008       ; First textbox that pops up automatically upon game start in the house
F13:0009       text1:

               S50:000A4F9D:  0B
